    <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"> athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"> svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām
                        anyabhāvitvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ
                        śuklatā raktānām anyavarṇatvaṃ sthirāṇāṃ mṛdutvaṃ mṛdūnāṃ sthiratā
                        calānām acalatvaṃ acalānāṃ calatā pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ
                        saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutā dīrghānāṃ hrasvatvaṃ hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā
                        apatanadharmiṇāṃ patanadharmitvaṃ patanadharmiṇāmapatanadharmitvaṃ
                        akasmāc ca śaityauṣṇyasnaigdhyaraukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇyāvasādanaṃ
                        cāṅgānām || svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasrastotkṣiptabhrāntāvakṣiptapatitavimuktanirgatāntargatagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇavyaṅgaprādurbhāvo vā'pyakasmāt sirāṇāṃ ca darśanaṃ
                        lalāṭe nāsāvaṃśe vā piḍakotpattiḥ lalāṭe prabhātakāle svedaḥ
                        netrarogād vinā vā'śrupravṛttiḥ gomayacūrṇaprakāśasya vā rajaso
                        darśanam uttamāṅge nilayanaṃ vā kapotakaṅkakākaprabhṛtīnāṃ
                        mūtrapurīṣavṛddhir abhuñjānānāṃ tatpraṇāśo bhuñjānānāṃ vā
                        stanamūlahṛdayor aḥsu ca śūlotpattayaḥ madhye śūnatvam anteṣu
                        parimlāyitvaṃ viparyayo vā tathā'rdhāṅge śvayathuḥ śoṣo
                        'ṅgapakṣayor vā naṣṭahīnavikalavikṛtasvaratā vā
                        vivarṇapuṣpaprādurbhāvo vā dantamukhanakhaśarīreṣu yasya vā'psu
                        kaphapurīṣaretāṃsi nimajjanti yasya vā dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni
                        rūpāṇy ālokyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti yaś ca durbalo
                        bhaktadveṣātisārābhyāṃ pīḍyate kāsamānaś ca tṛṣṇābhibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś
                        cchardibhaktadveṣayuktaḥ saphenapūyarudhirodvāmī hatasvaraḥ
                        śūlābhipannaś ca manuṣyaḥ śūnakaracaraṇavadanaḥ kṣīṇo 'nnadveṣī
                        srastapiṇḍikāṃsapāṇipādo jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ yas tu pūrvāhṇe
                        bhuktam aparāhṇe chardayaty avidagdham atisāryate vā
                        jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ sa śvāsān mriyate bastavad vilapan yaś ca
                        bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ stabdhameḍhro bhagnagrīvaḥ
                        pranaṣṭamehanaś ca manuṣyaḥ prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārdraśarīraḥ yaś
                        ca loṣṭaṃ loṣṭenābhihanti kāṣṭhaṃ kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā chinatti
                        adharoṣṭhaṃ daśati uttaroṣṭhaṃ vā leḍhi āluñcati vā karṇāu keśāṃś
                        ca devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyāṃś ca dveṣṭi yasya vakrānuvakragā grahā
                        garhitasthānagatāḥ pīḍayanti janmarkṣaṃ vā yasyolkāśanibhyām
                        abhihanyate horā vā
                        gṛhadāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5"> bhavanti cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsyamānaḥ samyak ca vikāro yo 'bhivardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabala<pc> </pc>māṃsasya lakṣaṇaṃ tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6"> nivartate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7"> etāny ariṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣāyāṃ sa rājñaḥ saṃmato bhavet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        svabhāvavipratipattirnāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ || </l>

                    <note ana="DW, 2022-04-10">From here on in the sūtrasthāna, MS
                        evidence is not available from witness K due to missing
                        folia.</note>
                </div>



                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1"> athāto 'vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3"> upadravais tu ye juṣṭā vyādhayo yānty avāryatām
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanād vinā vatsa tān śṛṇv ekamanā mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4"> vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭham arśo bhagandaram
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī mūḍhagarbhaś ca tathaivodaram aṣṭamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5"> aṣṭāv ete prakṛtyaiva duścikitsyā mahāgadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāṇamāṃsakṣayaśvāsatṛṣṇāśoṣavamījvaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6"> mūrcchātisārahikkābhiḥ punaś caitair upadrutāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         varjanīyā viśeṣeṇa bhiṣajā siddhim icchatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7"> śūnaṃ suptatvacaṃ bhagnaṃ kampādhmānanipīḍitam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraṃ rujārtamantaś ca vātavyādhir vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8"> yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         piḍakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9"> prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgaṃ ca raktanetraṃ
                        hatasvaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcakarmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hantīha kuṣṭhinam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10"> tṛṣṇārocakaśūlārtam atiprasrutaśoṇitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophātīsārasaṃyuktam arśovyādhir vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11"> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagandarāt prasravanti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12"> praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ ruddhamūtraṃ ruganvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī kṣapayatyāśu sikatāśarkarānvitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13"> garbhakoṣaparāsaṅgo makkallo yonisaṃvṛtiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyāt striyaṃ mūḍhagarbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14"> pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaśophātīsārapīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktaṃ pūryamāṇaṃ ca varjayed udarārditam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15"> yas tāmyati visaṃjñaś ca śete nipatito 'pi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītārdito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16"> yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūlavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         nityaṃ vaktreṇa cocchvasyāttaṃ jvaro hanti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17"> hikkāśvāsapipāsārtaṃ mūḍhaṃ vibhrāntalocanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayati jvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18"> āvilākṣaṃ pratāmyantaṃ nidrāyuktam atīva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaśoṇitamāṃsaṃ ca naraṃ nāśayati jvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19"> śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ kṣīṇaṃ jvaranipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddhamatīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20"> śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāramūrdhvaśvāsanipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛcchreṇa bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21"> śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣagranthimūḍhatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti durbalatvaṃ ca gulmino mṛtyumeṣyataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22"> ādhmātaṃ baddhaniṣyandaṃ chardihikkātṛḍanvitam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāśvāsasamāviṣṭaṃ vidradhirnāśayennaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23"> pāṇḍudantanakho yaś ca pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24"> lohitaṃ chardayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktānāṃ ca diśāṃ draṣṭā raktapittī vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25"> avāṅnukhastūnmukho vā kṣīṇamāṃsabalo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāgariṣṇur asandeham unmādena vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26"> bahuśo 'pasmarantaṃ tu prakṣīṇaṃ calitabhruvam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         netrābhyāṃ ca vikurvāṇam apasmāro vināśayet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne 'vāraṇīyo nāma
                        trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>



                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1"> athāto yuktasenīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3"> yuktasenasya nṛpateḥ parān abhijigīṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tad upadekṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4"> vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyair yātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣādeva narādhipaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5"> panthānam udakaṃ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasam
                        indhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dūṣayanty arayas tac ca jānīyāc chodhayet tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsā ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6"> ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatamatharvāṇaḥ pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣā āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7"> doṣāgantujamṛtyubhyo rasamantraviśāradau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣetāṃ nṛpatiṃ nityaṃ yattau vaidyapurohitau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8"> brahmā vedāṅgamaṣṭāṅgamāyurvedam abhāṣata |
                        <caesura/>
                         purohitamate tasmād varteta bhiṣag ātmavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9"> saṃkaraḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ praṇāśo dharmakarmaṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         prajānāmapi cocchittirnṛpavyasanahetutaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10"> puruṣāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca kevalaṃ tulyamūrtitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ājñā tyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyaṃ vikramaś cāpyamānuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11"> tasmād devamivābhīkṣṇaṃ vāṅnanaḥkarmabhiḥ
                        śubhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cintayennṛpatiṃ vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12"> skandhāvāre ca mahati rājagehādanantaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavetsannihito nityaṃ sarvopakaraṇānvitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13"> tatrasthamenaṃ
                        dhvajavadyaśaḥkhyātisamucchritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         upasarpantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārditāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14"> svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv
                        abahiṣkṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo dhvaja ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.15"> vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca bheṣajaṃ paricārakaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete pādāś cikitsāyāḥ karmasādhanahetavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16"> guṇavadbhis tribhiḥ pādaiś caturtho guṇavān
                        bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhimalpena kālena mahāntam api sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.17"> vaidyahīnāstrayaḥ pādā guṇavanto 'pyapārthakāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgātṛhotṛbrahmāṇo yathā'dhvaryuṃ vinā'dhvare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.18"> vaidyastu guṇavānekastārayed āturān sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         plavaṃ pratitarair hīnaṃ karṇadhāra ivāmbhasi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.19"> tattvād higataśāstrārtho dṛṣṭakarmā svayaṃkṛtī
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghuhastaḥ śuciḥ śūraḥ sajjopaskarabheṣajaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20"> pratyutpannamadtirdhīmān vyavasāyī viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         satyadharmaparo yaś ca sa bhiṣak pāda ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21"> āyuṣmān sattvavān sādhyo dravyavānātmavān api
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         āstiko vaidyavākyastho vyādhitaḥ pāda ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.22"> praśastadeśasaṃbhūtaṃ praśaste 'hani coddhṛtam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktamātraṃ manaskāntaṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.23"> doṣaghnamaglānikaramavikāri viparyaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         samīkṣya dattaṃ kāle ca bheṣajaṃ pāda ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.24"> snigdho 'jugupsur balavān yukto
                        vyādhitarakṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛdaśrāntaḥ pādaḥ paricaraḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yuktasenīyo nāma
                        catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>
                <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.1"> athātaḥ āturopakramaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.3"> āturam upakramamāṇena bhiṣajā+āyurādāveva
                        parīkṣitavyaṃ satyāyuṣi
                        vyādhyṛtvagnivayodehabalasattvasātmyaprakṛtibheṣajadeśān parīkṣeta
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.4"> tatra
                        mahāpāṇipādapārśvapṛṣṭhastanāgradaśanavadanaskandhalalāṭaṃ
                        dīrghāṅguliparvocchvāsaprekṣaṇabāhuṃ vistīrṇabhrūstanāntaroraskaṃ
                        hrasvajaṅghāmeḍhragrīvaṃ gambhīrasattvasvaranābhimanuccair
                        baddhastanam upacitamahāromaśakarṇaṃ paścān mastiṣkaṃ
                        srātānuliptaṃ mūrdhānupūrvyā viśuṣyamāṇaśarīraṃ paścāc ca
                        viśuṣyamāṇahṛdayaṃ puruṣaṃ jānīyād dīrghāyuḥ khalv ayam iti | tam
                        ekāntenopakramet | ebhir lakṣaṇair viparītair alpāyuḥ miśrair
                        madhyamāyur iti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.5"> bhavanti cātra | gūḍhasandhisirāsnāyuḥ
                        saṃhatāṅgaḥ sthirendriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttarottarasukṣetro yaḥ sa dīrghāyurucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.6"> garbhātprabhṛtyarogo yaḥ śanaiḥ sam upacīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrajñānavijñānaiḥ sa dīrghāyuḥ samāsataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.7"> madhyamasyāyuṣo jñānamata ūrdhvaṃ nibodha me |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhastādakṣayor yasya lekhāḥ syurvyaktamāyatāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.8"> dve vā tisro 'dhikā vā'pi pādau karṇau ca
                        māṃsalau |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāgram ūrdhvaṃ ca bhaved ūrdhvaṃ lekhāś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.9"> yasya syus tasya paramam āyur bhavati saptatiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         jaghany asyāyuṣo jñānam ata ūrdhvaṃ nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.10"> hrasvāni yasya parvāṇi sumahac cāpi mehanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathorasy avalīḍhāni na ca syāt pṛṣṭham āyatam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11"> ūrdhvaṃ ca śravaṇau sthānān nāsā coccā
                        śarīriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahato jalpato vā'pi dantamāṃsaṃ pradṛśyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11ef"> prekṣate yaś ca vibhrāntaṃ sa
                        jīvetpañcaviṃśatim || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12ab"> atha punar āyuṣo vijñānārthām
                        aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasārānupadekṣyāmaḥ | tatrāṅgāny
                        antarādhisakthibāhuśirāṃsi tadavayavāḥ pratyaṅgānīti | tatra svair
                        aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvyaṅgulāyate pradeśinyāstu
                        madhyāmānāmikākaniṣṭhikā yathottaraṃ pañcamabhāgahīnāḥ
                        catur{O.pañca}aṅgulāyate pañcāṅgulavistṛte</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12cd"> prekṣate yaś ca vibhrāntaṃ sa jīvet
                        pañcaviṃśatim || prapadapādatale pañcacaturaṅgulāyatavistṛtā
                        pārṣṇiḥ caturdaśāṅgulāyataḥ pādaḥ caturdaśāṅgulapariṇāhāni
                        pādagulphajaṅghājānumadhyāni aṣṭādaśāṅgulā jaṅghā jānūpariṣṭāc ca
                        dvātriṃśadaṅgulamevaṃ pañcāśat jaṅghāyāmasamāvūrū dvyaṅgulāni
                        vṛṣaṇacibukadaśananāsāpuṭabhāgadarṇamūlanayanāntarāṇi
                        caturaṅgulāni
                        mehanavadanāntaranāsākarṇalalāṭagrīvocchrāyadṛṣṭyantarāṇi
                        dvādaśāṅgulāni
                        bhagavistāramehananābhihṛdayagrīvāstanāntaramukhāyāmamaṇibandhaprakoṣṭhasthaulyāni
                        indrabastipariṇāhāṃsapīṭhakūrparāntarāyāmaḥ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaḥ
                        caturviṃśatyaṅgulo hastaḥ dvātriṃśadaṅgulaparimāṇau bhujau
                        dvātriṃśatpariṇāhāvūrū maṇibandhakūrparāntaraṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ talaṃ
                        ṣaṭcaturaṅgulāyāmavistāraṃ
                        aṅguṣṭhamūlapradeśinīśravaṇāpāṅgāntaramadhyamāṅgulyau pañcāṅgule
                        ardhapañcāṅgule pradeśinyanāmike sārdhatryaṅgulau kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhau
                        caturviṃśativistārapariṇāhaṃ mukhagrīvaṃ tribhāgāṅgulavistārā
                        nāsāpuṭamaryādā nayanatribhāgapariṇāhā tārakā navamas tārakāṃśo
                        dṛṣṭiḥ keśāntamastakāntaramekādaśāṅgulaṃ mastakādavaṭukeśānto
                        daśāṅgulaḥ karṇāvaṭvantaraṃ caturdaśāṅgulaṃ
                        puruṣoraḥpramāṇavistīrṇā strīśroṇiḥ aṣṭādaśāṅgulavistāramuraḥ
                        tatpramāṇā puruṣasya kaṭī saviṃśamaṅgulaśataṃ puruṣāyāma iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.13"> bhavanti cātra | pañcaviṃśe tato varṣe pumān
                        nārī tu ṣoḍaśe |
                        <caesura/>
                         samatvāgatavīryau tau jānīyāt kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.14"> dehaḥ svair aṅgulair eṣa yathāvad anukīrtitaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktaḥ pramāṇenānena pumān vā yadi vā'ṅganā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.15"> dīrgham āyur avāpnoti vittaṃ ca mahad ṛcchati
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhyamaṃ madhaymair āyur vittaṃ hīnais tathā'varam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.16ab"> atha sārān vakṣyāmaḥ
                        smṛtibhaktiprajñāśauryaśaucopetaṃ kalyāṇābhiniveṣaṃ sattvasāraṃ
                        vidyāt snigdhasaṃhataśvetāsthidantanakhaṃ bahulakāmaprajaṃ śukreṇa
                        akṛśam uttamabalaṃ snigdhagambhīrasvaraṃ saubhāgyopapannaṃ
                        mahānetraṃ ca majjñā mahāśiraḥskandhaṃ
                        dṛḍhadantahanvasthinakhamasthibhiḥ snigdhamūtrasvedasvaraṃ
                        bṛhaccharīramāyāsāsahiṣṇuṃ medasā acchidragātraṃ gūḍhāsthisandhiṃ
                        māṃsopacitaṃ ca māṃsena </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.16cd">
                        snigdhatāmranakhanayanatālujihvauṣṭhapāṇipādatalaṃ raktena
                        suprasannamṛdutvagromāṇaṃ tvaksāraṃ vidyād iti | eṣāṃ pūrvaṃ
                        pūrvaṃ pradhānam āyuḥsaubhāgyayor iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.17"> veśeṣato 'ṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇād atha sārataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         parīkṣyāyuḥ sunipuṇo bhiṣak sidhyati karmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.18"> vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāgabhihitāḥ sarva evaite
                        trividhāḥ sādhyā yāpyāḥ pratyākhyeyāś ca | tatraitān bhūyastridhā
                        parīkṣeta kimasāvaupasargikaḥ prākkevalo 'nyalakṣaṇa iti | tatra
                        aupasargiko yaḥ pūrvotpannaṃ vyādhiṃ jaghanyakālajāto
                        vyādhirupasṛjati sa tanmūla evopadravasaṃjñaḥ prākkevalo yaḥ
                        prāgevotpanno vyādhirapūrvarūpo 'nupadravaś ca anyalakṣaṇo yo
                        bhaviṣyad vyādhikhyāpakaḥ sa pūrvarūpasaṃjñaḥ | tatra sopadravam
                        anyonyāvirodhenopakrameta blavantam upadravaṃ vā prākkevalaṃ
                        yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta anyalakṣaṇe tv ādivyādhau prayateta || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.19"> bhavati cātra | nāsti rogo vinā doṣair yasmāt
                        tasmād vicakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anuktam api doṣāṇāṃ liṅgair vyādhim upācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.20"> prāgabhihitā ṛtavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.21"> śīte śītapratīkāram uṣṇe coṣṇanivāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtvā kuryāt kriyāṃ prāptāṃ kriyākālaṃ na hāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.22"> aprāpte vā kriyākāle prāpte vā na kṛtā kriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyā hīnā'tiriktā vā sādhyeṣv api na sidhyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.23"> yā hyudīrṇaṃ śamayati nānyaṃ vyādhiṃ karoti ca
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         sā kriyā na tu yā vyādhiṃ haraty anyam udīrayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.24"> prāgabhihito 'gnir annasya pācakaḥ | sa
                        caturvidho bhavati doṣānabhipanna ekaḥ vikriyām āpannas trividho
                        bhavati viṣamo vātena tīkṣṇaḥ pittena mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā caturtaḥ
                        samaḥ sarvasāmyād iti | tatra yo yathākālam upayuktam annaṃ samyak
                        pacati sa samaḥ samair doṣaiḥ yaḥ kadācit samyak pacati kāḍcid
                        ādhmānaśūlodāvartātisārajaṭharagauravāntrakūjanapravāhaṇāni kṛtvā
                        sa viṣamaḥ yaḥ prabhūtam apy upayuktamannamāśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ
                        sa evābhivardhamāno 'tyagnir ity abhāṣyate sa muhurmuhuḥ prabhūtam
                        apy upayuktam annam āśutaraṃ pacati pākānte ca
                        galatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpāñ janayati yastv alpam apy upayuktam
                        udaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsaprasekacchardigātrasadanāni kṛtvā mahatā
                        kālena pacati sa mandaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.25"> viṣamo vātajān rogāṃstīkṣṇaḥ pittanimittajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         karotyagnis tathā mando vikārān kaphasaṃbhavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.26"> tatra same parirakṣaṇaṃ kurvīta viṣame
                        snigdhāmlalavaṇaiḥ kriyāviśeṣaiḥ pratikurvīta tīkṣṇe
                        madhurasnigdhaśītair virekaiś ca evam evātyagnau viśeṣeṇa māhiṣaiś
                        ca kṣīradadhisarpirbhiḥ mande kaṭutiktakaṣāyair vamanaiś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.27"> jāṭharo bhagavānagnirīśvaro 'nnasya pācakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saukṣmyādrasānādadāno vivektuṃ naiva śakyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.28"> prāṇāpānasamānais tu sarvataḥ pavanais tribhiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhmāyate pācyate cāpi sve sve sthāne vyavasthitaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.29"> vayas tu trividhaṃ bālyaṃ madhyaṃ vṛddham iti
                        | tatronaṣoḍaśavarṣā bālāḥ | te 'pi trividhāḥ kṣīrapāḥ kṣīrānnādā
                        annādā iti | teṣu saṃvatsaraparāḥ kṣīrapāḥ dvisaṃvatsaraparāḥ
                        kṣīrānnādāh parato 'nnādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare madhyaṃ
                        vayaḥ | tasya vikalpo vṛddhiryauvanaṃ saṃpūrṇatā hānir iti | tatra
                        āviṃśatervṛddhiḥ ātriṃśate yauvanaṃ ācatvāriṃśataḥ
                        sarvadhātvindriyabalavīryasaṃpūrṇatā ata ūrdhvamīṣatparihāṇiryāvat
                        saptatir iti | saptaterūrdhvaṃ
                        kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyabalavīryotsāhamahanyahani
                        valīpalitakhālityajuṣṭaṃ kāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravair
                        abhibhūyamānaṃ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaṃ
                        jīrṇāgāramivābhivṛṣṭamavasīdantaṃ vṛddhamācakṣate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.30"> tatrottarottarāsu vayovasthāsūttarottarā
                        bheṣajamātrāviśeṣā bhavanti ṛte ca parihāṇeḥ tatrādyāpikṣayā
                        pratikurvīta || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.31"> bhavanti cātra | bāle vivardhate śleṣmā
                        madhyame pittam eva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vardhate vāyur vṛddhe tadvīkṣya yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.32"> agnikṣāravirekais tu bālavṛddhau vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatsādhyeṣu vikāreṣu mṛdvīṃ kuryāt kriyāṃ śanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.33"> dehaḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśo madhya iti prāgupadiṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.34"> karśayed bṛṃhayec cāpi sadā sthūlakṛśau narau
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣaṇaṃ caiva madhyasya kurvīta satataṃ bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.35"> balam abhihitaguṇaṃ daurbalyaṃ ca
                        svabhāvadeṣajarādibhir avekṣitavyam | yasmād balavataḥ
                        sarvakriyāpravṛttis tasmād balam eva pradhānam adhikaraṇānām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.36"> kecit kṛśāḥ prāṇavantaḥ sthūlāś cālpabalā
                        narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasmāt sthiratvavyāyāmair balaṃ vaidyaḥ pratarkayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.37"> sattvaṃ tu vyasanābhyudayakriyādisthāneṣu
                        aviklavakaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.38"> sattvavān sahate sarvaṃ saṃstabhyātmānam
                        ātamanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         rājasaḥ stabhyamāno 'nyaiḥ sahate naiva tāmasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.39"> sātmyāni tu
                        deśakālajātyṛturogavyāyāmodakadivāsvapnarasaprabhṛtīni
                        prakṛtiviruddhāny api yāny abādhakarāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.40"> yo rasaḥ kalpate yasya sukhāyaiva niṣevitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmajātamanyadvā tat sātmyam iti nirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.41"> prakṛtiṃ bheṣajaṃ copariṣṭādvakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.42"> deśastvānūpo jāṅgalaḥ sādhāraṇa iti | tatra
                        bahūdakanimnonnatanadīvarṣagahano mṛduśītānilo
                        bahumahāparvatavṛkṣo mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyaḥ
                        kaphavātarogabhūyiṣṭhaś cānupaḥ ākāśasamaḥ praviralālpa<pc
                        > </pc>kaṇṭakivṛkṣaprāyo 'lpavarṣaprasravaṇodapānodakāprāya
                        uṣṇadāruṇavāyaḥ praviralālpaśailaḥ sthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo
                        vātapittarogabhūyiṣṭhaś ca jāṅgalaḥ ubhayadeśalakṣaṇaḥ sādhāraṇa
                        iti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.43">bhavanti cātra | samāḥ sādhāraṇe
                        yasmācchītavarṣoṣmamārutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāṇāṃ samatā jantostasmāt sādhāraṇo mataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.44"> na tathā balavantaḥ syur jalajā vā sthalāhṛtāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         svadeśe nicitā doṣā anyasmin kopam āgatāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.45"> ucite vartamānasya nāsti deśakṛtaṃ bhayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau taddeśasya guṇe sati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.46"> deśaprakṛtisātmye tu viparīto 'cirotthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃpattau bhiṣagādīnāṃ balasattvāyuṣāṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.47"> kevalaḥ samadehāgneḥ sukhasādhyatamo gadaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ato 'nyathā tvasādhyaḥ syāt kṛcchro vyāmiśralakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.48"> kriyāyās tu guṇālābhe kriyām anyāṃ prayojayet
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvasyāṃ śantavegāyāṃ na kriyāsaṃkaro hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.49"> guṇālābhe 'pi sapadi yadi saiva kriyā hitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kartavyaiva tadā vyādhiḥ kṛcchrasādhyatamo yadi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.50"> ya evam enaṃ vidhim ekarūpaṃ bibharti
                        kālādivaśena dhīmān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa mṛtyupāśān jagato gadaughān chinatti bhaiṣajyaparaśvadhena || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āturopakramaṇīyo
                        nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhayāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ṣaḍtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
                    <!--<note xml:lang="en">There are large differences
                            between the Ācārya 1931 and 1938 editions version of
                            Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on this adhyāya.</note>-->

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1"> athāto bhūmipravibhāgīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3">
                        śvabhraśarkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghātanadevatāyatanasikatābhir
                        anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṅgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ
                        mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ samāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmimauṣadhārthaṃ
                        parīkṣeta | tasyāṃ jātamapi
                        kṛmiviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārgair
                        anupahatamekarasaṃ puṣṭaṃ pṛthvavagāḍhamūlamudīcyāṃ
                        cauṣadhamādadītetyeṣa bhūmiparīkṣāviśeṣaḥ sāmānyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4"> viśeṣatas tu tatra aśmavatī sthirā gurvī śyāmā
                        kṛṣṇā vā sthūlavṛkṣaśasyaprāyā svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā snigdhā
                        śītalā+āsannodakā snigdhaśasyatṛṇakomalavṛkṣaprāyā
                        śuklā'mbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā nānāvarṇā laghvaśmavatī
                        praviralālpapāṇḍuvṛkṣaprarohā'gniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā rūkṣā
                        bhasmarāsabhavarṇā
                        tanurūkṣakoṭarālparasavṛkṣaprāyā'nilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā mṛdvī samā
                        śvabhravatyavyaktarasajalā sarvato 'sāravṛkṣā
                        mahāparvatavṛkṣaprāyā śyāmā cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5"> atra kecid āhur ācāryāḥ
                        prāvṛḍvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ
                        mūlapatratvakkṣīrasāraphalāny ādadīteti tat tu na samyak
                        saumyāgneyatvāj jagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣv
                        ādadītāgneyāny āgneyeṣu evam avyāpannaguṇāni bhavanti | saumyāny
                        auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītāni somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau
                        jātāny atimadhurasnigdhaśītāni jāyante | etena śeṣaṃ vyākhyātam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6"> tatra pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni
                        virecanadravyāṇyādadīta agnyākāśamārutaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        vamanadravyāṇi ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām ubhayatobhāgāni
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāni evaṃ balavattarāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7"> sarvāṇyeva cābhinavāny anyatra
                        madhughṛtaguḍapippalīviḍaṅgebhyaḥ (ā.sarvāṇyeva sakṣīrāṇi
                        vīryavanti ) teṣām asampattāva(ā.na)tikrāntasaṃvatsarāṇy ādadīteti
                        || </l>

                <div n="37" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.1"> athāto miśrakam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.3"> mātuluṅgāgnimanthau ca bhadradāru mahauṣadham |
                        <caesura/>
                         ahiṃsrā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophajit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.4"> dūrvā ca nalamūlaṃ ca madhukaṃ candanaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalāś ca gaṇāḥ sarve pralepaḥ pittaśophahṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.5"> āgantuje raktaje ca hyeṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhir viṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'pi hitas tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.6"> ajagandhā'śvagandhā ca kālā saralayā saha |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaiṣikā'jaśrṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.7"> ete vargās trayo lodhraṃ pathyā piṇḍītakāni ca
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ sānnipātikaśophahṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.8"> snigdhāmlalavaṇo vāte koṣṇaḥ śītaḥ payoyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte coṣṇah kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.9"> śaṇamūlakaśigrūṇāṃ phalāni tilasarṣapāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaktavaḥ kiṇvamatasī dravyāṇyuṣṇāni pācanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10"> cirabilvo 'gniko dantī citrako hayamārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kapotagṛdhrakaṅkāṇāṃ purīṣāṇi ca dāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāradravyāṇi vā yāni kṣāro vā dāraṇaṃ param || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.11"> dravyāṇāṃ picchilānāṃ tu tvaṅnūlāni prapīḍanam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         yavagodhūmamāṣāṇāṃ cūrṇāni ca samāsataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.12"> śaṅkhinyaṅkoṭhasumanaḥkaravīrasuvarcalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni kaṣāyāṇi vargaś cāragvadhādikaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.13"> ajagandhā'jaśṛṅgī ca gavākṣī lāṅgalāhvayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūtīkaś citrakaḥ pāṭhā viḍaṅgailāhareṇavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.14"> kaṭutrikaṃ yavakṣāro lavaṇāni manaḥśilā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsaṃ trivṛtā dantī haritālaṃ surāṣṭrajā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.15"> saṃśodhanīnāṃ vartīnāṃ dravyāṇy etāni nirdiśet
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair evauṣadhaiḥ kuryāt kalkān api ca śodhanān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16ab"> kāsīsakaṭurohiṇyor jātīkandaharidrayoḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16cd"> pūrvoddiṣṭeṣu cāṅgeṣu kuryāt tailaghṛtāni
                        vai || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.17"> arkottamāṃ snuhīkṣīraṃ piṣṭvā kṣārottamān api
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         jātīmūlaṃ haridre dve kāsīsaṃ kaṭurohiṇīm || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18ab"> pūrvoddiṣṭāni cānyāni kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ
                        ghṛtam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18cd"> mayūrako rājavṛkṣo nimbaḥ kośātakī tilāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.19"> bṛhatī kaṇṭakārī ca haritālaṃ manaḥśilā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni ca yojyāni taile dravyāṇi śodhane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.20"> kāsīse saindhave kiṇve vacāyāṃ rajanīdvaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāṅgeṣu cānyeṣu cūrṇaṃ kurvīta śodhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.21"> sālasārādisāreṣu paṭolatriphalāsu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyā vidhātavyā śodhanī śodhaneṣu ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.22"> śrīveṣṭake sarjarase sarale devadāruṇi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāreṣv api ca kurvīta matimān vraṇadhūpanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.23"> kaṣāyāṇāmanuṣṇānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ tvakṣu sādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛtaṃ śītaṃ kaṣāyaṃ vā ropaṇārtheṣu śasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.24"> somāmṛtāśvagandhāsu kākolyādau gaṇe tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīripraroheṣv api ca vartayo ropaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.25"> samaṅgā somasaralā somavalkaḥ sacandanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādiś ca kalkaḥ syāt praśasto vraṇaropaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.26"> pṛthakparṇyātmaguptā ca haridre mālatī sitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādiś ca yojyaḥ syādbhiṣajā ropaṇe ghṛte || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.27"> kālānusāryāguruṇī haridre devadāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgavaś ca rodhraṃ ca taile yojyāni ropaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.28"> kaṅgukā triphalā rodhraṃ kāsīsaṃ śravaṇāhvayā
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavāśvakarṇayos tvak ca ropaṇaṃ cūrṇam iṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.29"> priyaṅgukā sarjarasaḥ puṣpakāsīsam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvakcūrṇaṃ dhavajaṃ caiva ropaṇārthaṃ praśasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.30"> tvakṣu nyagrodhavargasya triphalāyāstathaiva
                        ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyāṃ ropaṇārthe vidadhīta yathākramam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.31"> apāmārgo 'svagandhā ca tālapatrī suvarcalā |
                        <caesura/>
                         utsādane praśasyante kākolyādiś ca yo gaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.32"> kāsīsaṃ saindhavaṃ kiṇvaṃ kuruvindo manaḥśilā
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         kukkuṭāṇḍakapālāni sumanomukulāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33ab"> phale śairīṣakārañje dhātucūrṇāni yāni ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33cd"> vraṇeṣūtsannamāṃseṣu praśastāny avasādane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.34"> samastaṃ vargam ardhaṃ vā yathālābham athāpi
                        vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājño yathoddiṣṭeṣu karmasu || </l>

                        nāma saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekonacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.1"> athātaḥ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.3">
                        madanakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārgavakṛtavedhanasarṣapaviḍaṅgapippalīkarañjaprapunnāḍakovidārakarbudārāriṣṭāśvagandhāvidulabandhujīvakaśvetāśaṇapuṣpībimbīvacāmṛgervāruś
                        citrā cety ūrdhvabhāgaharāṇi | tatra kovidārapūrvāṇāṃ phalāni
                        kovidārādīnāṃ mūlāni || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.4">
                        vivṛtāśyāmādantīdravantīsaptalāśaṅkhinīviṣāṇikāgavākṣīcchagalāntrīsruksuvarṇakṣīrīcitrakakiṇihīkuśakāśatilvakakampillakaramyakapāṭalāpūgaharītakyāmalakabibhītakanīlinīcaturaṅgulair
                        aṇḍapūtīkamahāvṛkṣasaptacchadārkā jyotiṣmatī cety adhobhāgaharāṇi
                        | tatra tilvakapūrvāṇāṃ mūlāni tilvakādīnāṃ pāṭalāntānāṃ tvacaḥ
                        kampillakaphalarajaḥ pūgādīnām eraṇḍāntānāṃ phalāni
                        pūtīkāragvadhayoḥ patrāṇi śeṣāṇāṃ kṣīrāṇīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.5"> koṣātakī saptalā śaṅkhinī devadālī kāravellikā
                        cety ubhayatobhāgaharāṇi | eṣāṃ svarasā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.6">
                        pippalīviḍaṅgāpāmārgaśigrusiddhārthakaśirīṣamaricakaravīrabimbīgirikarṇikākiṇihīvacājyotiṣmatīkarañjārkālarkalaśunātiviṣāśṛṅgaveratālīśatamālasurasārjakeṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgukīmeṣaśṛṅgīmātuluṅgīsuraṅgīpīlujātīśālatālamadhūkalākṣāhiṅgulavaṇamadyagośakṛdrasamūtrāṇīti
                        śirovirecanāni | tatra karavīrapūrvāṇāṃ phalāni
                        karavīrādīnāmarkāntānāṃ mūlāni tālīśapūrvāṇāṃ kandāḥ
                        tālīśādīnāmarjakāntānāṃ patāṇi iṅgukīmeṣaśṛṅgyostavacaḥ
                        mātuluṅgīsuraṅgīpīlujātīnāṃ pūspāṇi śālatālamadhūkānāṃ sārāḥ
                        hiṅgulākṣe niryāsau lavaṇāni pārthivaviśeṣāḥ madyāny āsutasaṃyogāḥ
                        śakṛdrasamūtre malāv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.7"> saṃśamanāny ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra
                        bhadradārukuṣṭhaharidrāvaruṇameṣaśrṅgībalātibalārtagalakacchurāsallakīkuberākṣīvīratarusahacarāgnimanthavatsādanyeraṇḍāśmabhedakālarkārkaśatāvarīpunarnavāvasukavaśirakāñcanakabhārgīkārpāsīvṛścikālīpattūrabadarayavakolakulatthaprabhṛtīni
                        vidārigandhādiś ca dve cādye pañcamūlyau samasena vātasaṃśamano
                        vargaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.8">
                        candanakucandanahrīverośīramañjiṣṭhāpayasyādidārīśatāvarīgundrāśaivalakahlārakumudotpalakanda(ā.da)līdūrvāmūrvāprabhṛtīni
                        kākolyādiḥ sārivādirañjanādirutpalādirnyagrodhādistṛṇapañcamūlam
                        iti samāsena pittasaṃśamano vargaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.9">
                        kāleyakāgurutilaparṇīkuṣṭhaharidrāśītaśivaśatapuṣpāsaralārāsnāprakīryodakīryeṅgudīsumanaḥkākādanīlāṅgalakīhastikarṇamuñjātakalāmajjakaprabhṛtīni
                        vallīkaṇṭakapañcamūlyau pippalyādirbṛhatyādirmuṣkakādirvacādiḥ
                        surasādirāragvadhādir iti samāsena śleṣmasaṃśamano vargaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.10"> tatra sarvāṇy evauṣadhāni
                        vyādhyagnipuruṣabalānyam{??}isamīkṣya vidadhyāt | tatra
                        vyādhibalādadhikamauṣadham upayuktaṃ tam upaśamya vyādhiṃ
                        vyādhimanyamāvahati agnibalādadhikamajīrṇaṃ viṣṭabhya vā pacyate
                        puruṣabalādadhikaṃ glānimūrcchāmadānāvahati saṃśamanaṃ evaṃ
                        saṃśodhanam atipātayati | hīnamebhyo dattam akiṃcitkaraṃ bhavati |
                        tasmāt samam eva vidadhyāt || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11"> bhavanti cātra |

                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhaved alpabalasyāpi prayuktaṃ vyādhināśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.14"> vyādhyādiṣu tu madhyeṣu kvāthasyāñjalir iṣyate

                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhayāyaḥ /</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1"> athāto dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākavijñānīyam
                        adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3"> kecid ācāryā bruvate dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ kasmāt
                        vyavasthitatvāt iha khalu dravyaṃ vyavasthitaṃ na rasādayaḥ yathā
                        āme phale ye rasādayaste pakve na santi nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi
                        dravyamanityā guṇāḥ yathā kalkādipravibhāgaḥ sa eva
                        saṃpannarasagandho vyāpannarasagandho vā bhavati
                        svajātyavasthānācca yathā hi pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvaṃ na
                        gacchatyevaṃ śeṣāṇi pañcendriyagrahaṇāc ca pañcabhir indriyair
                        gṛhyate dravyaṃ na rasādayaḥ āśrayatavāc ca dravyam āśritā
                        rasādayo bhavanti ārambhasāmarthyāc ca dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ yathā
                        vidārigandhādimāhṛtya saṃkṣudya vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣv
                        ārambhaḥ śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstre hi dravyaṃ pradhānam upadeśe hi
                        yogānāṃ yathā mātuluṅgāgnimanthau cetyādau na rasādaya upadiśyante
                        kramāpekṣitatvāc ca rasādīnāṃ rasādayo hi dravyakramam apekṣante
                        yathā taruṇe taruṇāḥ saṃpūrṇe saṃpūrṇā iti ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca
                        dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante yathā mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti
                        tasmād dravyaṃ pradhānam | dravyalakṣaṇaṃ tu kriyāguṇavat
                        samavāyikāraṇam iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4"> nety āhur anye rasās tu pradhānaṃ kasmāt āgamāt
                        āgamo hi śāstram ucyate śāstre hi rasā adhikṛtāḥ yathā rasāyatta
                        āhāra iti tasmiṃś ca prāṇāḥ upadeśāc ca upadiśyante hi rasāḥ yathā
                        madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti anumānāc ca rasena hyanumīyate
                        dravyaṃ yathā madhuram iti ṛṣivacanāc ca ṛṣivacanaṃ vedo yathā
                        kiṃcid ijyārthaṃ madhuram āhared iti tasmād rasāḥ pradhānaṃ raseṣu
                        guṇasaṃjñā | rasalakṣaṇam anyatropadekṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5"> nety āhur anye vīryaṃ pradhānam iti | kasmāt
                        tad vaśenauṣadhakarmaniṣpatteḥ | ihauṣadhakarmāṇy
                        ūrdhvādhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṃgrāhakāgnidīpanapīḍanalekhanabṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaśvayathukaravilayanadahanadāraṇamādanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni
                        vīryaprādhānyād bhavanti | tac ca vīryaṃ dvividham uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ ca
                        agnīṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ śītam uṣṇaṃ
                        snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ viśadaṃ piccilaṃ mṛdu tīkṣṇaṃ ceti | etāni vīryāṇi
                        svabalaguṇotkarṣādrasamabhibhūyātmakarma kurvanti | yathā tāvan
                        mahatpañcamūlaṃ kaṣāyaṃ tiktānurasaṃ vātaṃ śamayati uṣṇavīryatvāt
                        tathā kulatthāḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭukaḥ palāṇḍuḥ snehabhāvāc ca madhuraś
                        cekṣuraso vātaṃ vardhayati śītavīryatvāt kaṭukā pippalī pittaṃ
                        śamayati mṛduśītavīryatvāt amlamāmalakaṃ lavaṇaṃ saidhavaṃ ca
                        tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ vardhayati uṣṇavīryatvāt madhurā matsyāśca
                        kaṭukaṃ mūlakaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ śamayati rūkṣavīryatvāt madhuraṃ
                        kṣaudraṃ ca tad etan nidarśanamātram uktam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6"> bhavanti cātra | ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti
                        yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         raukṣyalāghavaśaityāni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7"> ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutāś caiva na te tat karmakāriṇaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8"> ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaityāni na te tatkarmakāriṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9"> tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10"> nety āhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt
                        samyaṅnithyāvipākatvāt iha sarvadravāṇy{O.vyāṇy}abhyavahṛtāni
                        samyaṅnithyāvipakvāni guṇaṃ doṣaṃ vā janayanti | tatr āhur anye
                        prati rasaṃ pāka iti | kecittrividhamicchanti madhuramamlaṃ
                        kaṭukaṃ ceti | tattu na samyak bhūtaguṇād āmāc cānyo 'mlo vipāko
                        nāsti pittaṃ hi vidagdham amlatām upaity agner mandatvāt yady evaṃ
                        lavaṇo 'py anyaḥ pāko bhaviṣyanti śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām
                        upaitīti | madhuro madhurasyāmlo 'mlasyaivaṃ sarveṣām iti kecid
                        āhuḥ dṛṣṭāntaṃ copadiśanti yathā tāvat kṣīramukhāgataṃ pacyamānaṃ
                        madhuram eva syāt tathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam
                        uttarakāle 'pi na parityajanti tadvaditi | kecid vadanti
                        abalavanto balavatāṃ vaśam āyāntīti | evam anavasthitiḥ tasmād
                        asiddhānta eṣaḥ | āgame hi dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca |
                        tayor madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyaṃ bhavati guṇasādharmyād
                        gurutā laghutā ca pṛthivyāpaś ca gurvyaḥ śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād
                        dvividha eva pāka iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11"> bhavanti cātra | dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv
                        ambupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirvartante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12"> tejo 'nilākāśaguṇāḥ pacyamāneṣu yeṣu tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirvartante 'dhikās tatra pākaḥ kaṭuka ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13"> pṛthaktvadarśinām eṣa vādināṃ vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         catruṇāmapi sāmagryam icchanty atra vipaścitaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14"> tad dravyam ātmanā kiṃcit kiṃcid vīryeṇa
                        sevitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiṃcid rasavipākābhyāṃ doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15"> pāko nāsti vinā vīryādvīryaṃ nāsti vinā rasāt
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         raso nāsti vinā dravyāddravyaṃ śreṣṭhataṃ smṛtam || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16"> janma tu dravyarasayoranyonyāpekṣikaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syāddehadehinoḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17"> vīryasaṃjñā guṇā ye 'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ
                        smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāstu guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18"> dravye dravyāṇi yasmād dhi vipacyante na
                        ṣaḍrasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śreṣṭhaṃ dravyam ato jñeyaṃ śeṣā bhāvās tadāśrayāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19"> amīmāṃsyāny acintyāni prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20"> pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalāḥ prasiddhāś ca
                        svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nauṣadhīr hetubhir vidvān parīkṣeta kathaṃ(ā.dā)cana || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21"> sahasroṇāpi hetūnāṃ nāmbaṣṭhādir virecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tiṣṭhet tu matim ānāgame na tu hetuṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyaṃ sūtrasthāne
                        dravyaguṇarasavīryavipākavijñānīyo nāma catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        || </l>



                </div>

                <div n="41" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.1"> athāto dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3"> tatra pṛthivy<pc> </pc>aptejo<pc
                        > </pc>vāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyād dravyābhinirvṛttiḥ utkarṣas tv
                        abhivyājñjalo bhavati idaṃ pārthivam idam āpyam idaṃ taijasam idaṃ
                        vāyavyam idam ākāśīyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1"> tatra sthūla<pc> </pc>sāra<pc
                            > </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>sthira<pc
                            > </pc>guru<pc> </pc>kaṭhinaṃ gandha<pc> </pc>bahulam
                        īṣatkaṣāyaṃ prāyaśo madhuram iti pārthivaṃ tat sthairya<pc
                            > </pc>bala<pc> </pc>gaurava<pc> </pc>saṃghātopacaya<pc
                        > </pc>karaṃ viśeṣataś cādhogatisvabhāvam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2"> śīta<pc> </pc>stimita<pc
                            > </pc>snigdha<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>guru<pc
                            > </pc>sara<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>mṛdu<pc> </pc>picchilaṃ
                        rasabahulam īṣatkaṣāyāmlalavaṇaṃ madhurarasaprāyam āpyaṃ tat
                        snehanahlādanakledanabandhanaviṣyandanakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3"> uṣṇatīkṣṇasūkṣmarūkṣakharalaghuviśadaṃ
                        rūpa(ā.guṇa)bahulamīṣadamlalavaṇaṃ kaṭukarasaprāyaṃ viśeṣataś
                        cordhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ
                        taddahanapacanadāraṇatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4"> sūkṣmarūkṣakharaśiśiralaghuviśadaṃ
                        sprarśabahulamīṣattiktaṃ viśeṣataḥ kaṣāyam iti vāyavīyaṃ
                        tadvaiśadyalāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇavicāraṇakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5">
                        ślakṣṇasūkṣmamṛduvyavāyiviśadaviviktamavyaktarasaṃ
                        śabdabahulamākāśīyaṃ tanmārdavaśauṣiryalāghavakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5"> anena nidarśanena nānauṣadhībhūtaṃ jagati
                        kiṃcid dravyam astīti kṛtvā taṃ taṃ yuktiviśeṣamarthaṃ
                        cābhisamīkṣya svavīryaguṇayuktāni dravyāṇi kārmukāṇi bhavanti |
                        tāni yadā kurvanti sa kālaḥ yat kurvanti tat karma yena kurvanti
                        tad vīryaṃ yatra kurvanti tad adhikaranaṃ yathā kurvanti sa upāyaḥ
                        yan niṣpādayanti tat phalam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6"> tatra virecanadravyāṇi
                        pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni pṛthivyāpo gurvyastā gurutvād adho
                        gacchanti tasmād virecanam adhoguṇabhūyiṣṭham anumānāt
                        vamanadravyāṇy agnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni agnivāyū hi laghū laghutvāc
                        ca tāny ūrdhvam uttiṣṭhanti tasmād vamanam apy
                        ūrdhvaguṇabhūyiṣṭham ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭham ubhyato bhāgam
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ sāṃgrāhikam anilaguṇabhūyiṣṭham
                        anilasya śoṣaṇātmakatvāt dīpanam agniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ (?
                        tatsamānatvāt ) lekhanam anilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ
                        pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭham evam auṣadhakarmāṇy anumānāt sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7"> bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūtejovārijair dravyaiḥ śamaṃ yāti samīraṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittaṃ kṣipram āpnoti nirvṛtim || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8"> khatejonilajaiḥ śleṣmā śamam eti śarīriṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         viyatpavanajātābhyāṃ vṛddhim āpnoti mārutaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9"> āgneyam eva yad dravyaṃ tena pittam udīryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vasudhājalajātābhyāṃ balāsaḥ parivardhate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10"> evam etad guṇādhikyaṃ dravye dravye viniścitam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviśo vā bahuśo vā'pi jñātvā doṣeṣu cācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11"> tatra ya ime guṇā vīryasaṃjñakāḥ
                        śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviśadās teṣāṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇāv
                        āgneyau śītapicchilāv ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ
                        snehaḥ toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ mṛdutvaṃ vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ
                        kṣitisamīraṇaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vaiśadyaṃ gurulaghuvipākāv uktaguṇau
                        tatra uṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ
                        tīkṣnarūkṣaviśadāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ laghupākaḥ
                        śleṣmaghnaḥ teṣāṃ mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ picchalaviśadau
                        cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ snigdharūkṣau cakṣuṣā tīkṣṇo mukhaduḥkhotpādanāt
                        gurupākaḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphotkleśena ca laghur
                        baddhaviṇmūtratayā mārutakopena ca | tatra tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu
                        rasavaiśeṣyam upalakṣayet tadyathā madhuro guruś ca pārthivaḥ
                        madhuraḥ snigdhaś cāpya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12"> bhavati cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇā ya uktā dravyeṣu śarīreṣv api te tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānavṛddhikṣayās tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyo nāmaikacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>


                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvicatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1"> athāto rasaviśeṣavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3"> ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam
                        ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ śabdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ tasmād āpyo rasaḥ |
                        parasparasaṃsargāt parasparānugrahāt parasparānupraveśāc ca
                        sarveṣu sarveṣāṃ sānnidhyam asti utkarṣāpakarṣāt tu grahaṇam | sa
                        khalv āpyo rasaḥ śeṣabhūtasaṃsargād vidagdhaḥ ṣoḍhā vibhajyate
                        tadyathā madhuro 'mlo lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ kaṣāya iti | te ca
                        bhūyaḥ parasparasaṃsargāt triṣaṣṭidhā bhidyante | tatra
                        bhūmyambuguṇabāhulyān madhuraḥ bhūmyagniguṇabāhulyād amlaḥ
                        toyāgniguṇabāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvagniguṇabāhulyāt kaṭukaḥ
                        vāyvākāśaguṇabāhulyāt tiktaḥ pṛthivyanilaguṇabāhulyāt kaṣāya iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4"> tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ
                        madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pitaghnāḥ kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5"> tatra vāyo(āyu)rātmaivātmā pittam āgneyaṃ
                        śleṣmā saumya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6"> ta ete rasāḥ svayonivardhanā anyayonipraśamanāś
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7"> kecid āhur agnīṣomīyatvāj jagato rasā dvividhāḥ
                        saumyā āgneyāś ca | tatra madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ saumyāḥ
                        kaṭvamlalavaṇā āgneyāḥ | tatra madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ snigdhā guravaś
                        ca kaṭutiktakaṣāyā rūkṣā laghavaś ca saumyāḥ śītā āgneyāś coṣṇāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1"> tatra
                        śaityaraukṣyalāghavavaiśadyavaiṣṭambhyaguṇalakṣaṇo vāyuḥ tasya
                        samānayoniḥ kaṣāyo rasaḥ so 'sya śaityācchaityaṃ vardhayati
                        raukṣyādraukṣyaṃ lāghavāllāghavaṃ vaiśadyādvaiśadyaṃ
                        vaiṣṭambhyādvaiṣṭambhyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2">
                        auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiśadyaguṇalakṣaṇaṃ pittaṃ tasya
                        samānayoniḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ so 'syauṣṇyādauṣṇaṃ vardhayati
                        taikṣṇyāttaikṣṇyaṃ raukṣyādraukṣyaṃ lāghavāllāghavaṃ
                        vaiśadyādvaiśadyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3">
                        mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā tasya
                        samānayonirmadhuro rasaḥ so 'sya mādhuryānmādhuryaṃ vardhayati
                        snehāt snehaṃ gauravād gauravaṃ śaityācchaityaṃ
                        paicchilyātpaicchilyam iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8"> {ṃ.4} tasya punaranyoniḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ sa
                        śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt kaṭukatvānmādhuryamabhibhavati raukṣyāt
                        snehaṃ lāghavād gauravamauṣṇyācchaityaṃ vaiśadyātpaicchilyam iti |
                        tadetannidarśanamātramuktam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9"> rasalakṣaṇamata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra yaḥ
                        paritoṣamutpādayati prahlādayati tarpayati jīvayati
                        mukho{O.ā}palepaṃ janayati śleṣmāṇaṃ cābhivardhayati sa madhuraḥ
                        yo dantaharṣamutpādayati mukhāsrāvaṃ janayati śraddhāṃ cotpādayati
                        so 'mlaḥ yo bhaktarucimutpādayati kaphaprasekaṃ janayati mārdavam
                        cāpādayati sa lavaṇaḥ yo jihvāgraṃ bādhate udvegaṃ janayati śiro
                        gṛhṇīte nāsikāṃ ca srāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ yo gale coṣamutpādayati
                        mukhavaiśadyaṃ janayati bhaktaruciṃ cāpādyati harṣaṃ ca sa tiktaḥ
                        yo vaktraṃ pariśoṣayati jihvāṃ stambhayati kaṇṭhaṃ badhnāti
                        hṛdayaṃ karṣati pīḍayati ca sa kaṣāyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1"> rasaguṇānata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra madhuro
                        raso rasaraktamāṃsamedo 'sthimajjaujaḥśukrastanyavardhanaś
                        cakṣuṣyaḥ keṣyo varṇyo balakṛtsandhānaḥ śoṇitarasaprasādano
                        bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ
                        ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhapraśamanaḥ
                        ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaḥ kṛmikaphakaraś ceti sa evaṃguṇo 'pyeka
                        evātyarthamāsevyamānaḥ
                        kāsaśvāsālasakavamathuvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍānāpādayati
                        tathā'rbudaślīpadabastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtīñjanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2"> amlo jaraṇaḥ pācano dīpanaḥ pavananigrahaṇo
                        'nulomanaḥ koṣṭhavidāhī bahiḥśītaḥ kledanaḥ prāyaśo hṛdyaś ceti sa
                        evaṃguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        dantaharṣanayanasaṃmīlanaromasaṃvejanakaphavilayanaśarīraśaithilyānyāpādyati
                        tathā
                        kṣatābhihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnaśūnarugṇapracyutāvamūtritavisarpitacchinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
                        pācayatyāgneyasvabhāvāt paridahati kaṇṭhamuro hṛdayaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3"> lavaṇaḥ saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇaḥ
                        kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛduṣṇaḥ sarvarasapratyanīko mārgaviśodhanaḥ
                        sarvaśarīrāvayavamārdavakaraś ceti sa evaṃguṇo 'pyeka
                        evātyarthamāsevyamāno
                        gātrakaṇḍūkoṭhaśophavaivarṇyapuṃstvopaghātendriyopatāpamukhākṣipākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlakāprabhṛtīnāpādayati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4"> kaṭuko dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ
                        sthaulyālasyakaphakṛmiviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpaśamanaḥ
                        sandhibandhavicchedano 'vasādnaḥ stanyaśukramedasām upahantā ceti
                        sa evaṃguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasaṃtāpabalavighātakampatodabhedakṛt
                        karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlānāpādayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5"> tiktaś chedano rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ
                        kaṇḍūkoṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchājvarapraśamanaḥ stanyaśodhano
                        viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaś ceti sa evaṃguṇo 'pyeka
                        evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        gātramanyāstambhākṣepakārditaśiraḥśūlabhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyānyāpādayati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6"> {ṃ.6} kaṣāyaḥ saṃgrāhako ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ
                        śodhano lekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti sa evaṃguṇo
                        'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
                        hṛtpīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambhagātrasphuraṇacumucumāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtīñjanayati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11"> ataḥ sarveṣāmeva dravyāṇyupadekṣyāmaḥ |
                        tadyathā kākolyādiḥ
                        kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukatrapusair
                        vārukarkārukālāvukālindakatakagiloḍyapiyālapuṣkarabījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādanatālanālikerekṣuvikārabalātibalātmaguptāvidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena madhuro vargaḥ
                        dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrātakakapitthakaramardabadarakollaprācīnāmalakatintiḍīkakośāmrakabhavyapārāvatavetraphalalakucāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāśuktasauvīrakatuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsenāmlo vargaḥ
                        saindhavasauvarcalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrakapaktrimayavakṣāroṣaraprasūtasuvarcikāprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena lavaṇo vargaḥ pippalyādiḥ surasādiḥ
                        śigrumadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukāvalgujaphalacaṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsāpīluprabhṛtīni
                        sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko vargaḥ
                        āragvadhādirguḍūcyādirmaṇḍūkaparṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇabṛhatīdvayaśaṅkhinīdravantītrivṛtkṛtavedhanakarkoṭakakāravellavārtākakarīrakaravīrasumanaḥśaṅkhapuṣpyapāmārgatrāyamāṇā'śokarohiṇīvaijayantīsuvarcalāpunarnavāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena tikto vargaḥ nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādiḥ priyaṅvādī
                        rodhrādistriphalā śallakījambvāmrabakulatindukaphalāni
                        katakaśākapāṣāṇabhedakavanaspatiphalāni sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ
                        kuruvakakovidārakajīvantīcillīpālaṅkyāsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni
                        nīvārakādayo mudgādayaś ca vaidalāḥ samāsena kaṣāyo vargaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12"> tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogās triṣaṣṭir
                        bhavanti | tad yathā pañcadaśa dvikāḥ viṃśatis trikāḥ pañcadaśa
                        catuṣkāḥ ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ ekaśaḥ ṣaḍrasāḥ ekaḥ ṣaṭka iti | teṣām
                        anyatra prayojanāni vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13"> bhavati cātra | jagdhāḥ ṣaḍadhigacchanti
                        balino vaśatāṃ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā prakupitā doṣā vaśaṃ yānti balīyasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        rasaviśeṣavijñānīyo nāma dvācatravāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>



                <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1"> athāto vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part1"> vamanadravyāṇāṃ phalādīnāṃ madanaphalāni
                        śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti | atha madanapuṣpāṇāmātapapariśuṣkāṇāṃ
                        cūrṇaprakuñcaṃ pratyakpuṣpāsadāpuṣpīnimbakaṣāyāṇāmanyatamenāloḍya
                        madhusaindhavayuktāṃ puṣpacūrṇamātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        madanaśalāṭucūrṇāny evaṃ vā bakularamyakopayuktāni
                        madhulavaṇayuktāny abhiprataptāni madanaśalāṭucūrṇasiddhāṃ vā
                        tilataṇḍulayavāgūm | nirvṛttānāṃ vā nātiharitapāṇḍūnāṃ
                        kuśamūḍhāvabaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavatuṣamudgamāṣaśālyādidhāny arāśāvaṣṭarātroṣitaklinnabhinnānāṃ
                        phalānāṃ phalapippalīruddhṛtyātape śoṣayet tāsāṃ
                        dadhimadhupalalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ
                        subhājanasthānāmantarnakhamuṣṭimuṣṇe yaṣṭīmadhukakaṣāye
                        kovidārādīnāmanyatame vā kaṣāye pramṛdya rātriparyuṣitaṃ
                        madhusaindhavayuktamāśīrbhir abhimantritamudaṅnukhaḥ
                        prāṅnukhamāturaṃ pāyayed anena mantreṇābhimantrya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1"> brahmadakṣāśvirudrendrabhūcandrārkānalānilāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu te || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.2"> rasāyanamivarṣīṇāṃ devānām amṛtaṃ yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudhevottamanāgānāṃ bhaiṣajyamidamas tu te ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part2"> viśeṣeṇa
                        śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvidradhiṣu apravartamāne vā doṣe
                        pippalīvacāgaurasarṣapakalkonmiśraiḥ salavaṇais tuṣāmbubhiḥ punaḥ
                        punaḥ pravartayed āsamyagvāntalakṣaṇād iti |
                        madanaphalamajjacūrṇaṃ vā tatkvāthaparibhāvitaṃ
                        madanaphalakaṣāyeṇa madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payasaḥ
                        santānikāṃ kṣaudrayuktāṃ madanaphalamajjasiddhaṃ vā payaḥ
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā yavāgūm
                        adhobhāgāsṛkpittahṛddāhayoḥ madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso
                        dadhibhāvam upagatasya dadhyuttaraṃ dadhi vā
                        kaphaprasekacchardimūrcchātamakeṣu madanaphalamajjarasaṃ
                        bhallātakasnehavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet ātapapariśuṣkaṃ vā
                        tameva jīvantīkaṣāyeṇa pitte kaphasthānagate
                        madanaphalamajjakvāthaṃ vā pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ taccūrṇaṃ vā
                        nimbarūpikākaṣāyayor anyatareṇa saṃtarpaṇakaphajavyādhiharaṃ
                        madanaphalamajjacūrṇaṃ vā madhukakāśmaryadrākṣākaṣāyeṇa |
                        madanaphalavidhānam uktam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4"> jīmūtakakusumacūrṇaṃ pūrvavadeva kṣīreṇa
                        nirvṛtteṣu kṣīrayavāgūṃ romaśeṣu santānikāṃ aromaśeṣu dadhyuttaraṃ
                        haritapāṇḍuṣu dadhi tatkaṣāyasaṃsṛṣṭāṃ vā surāṃ
                        kaphārocakakāsaśvāsapāṇḍurogayakṣmasu paryāgateṣu
                        madanaphalamajjavadupayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5"> tadvad eva kuṭajaphalavidhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"> kṛtavedhanānām apy eṣa eva kalpaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7"> ikṣvākukusumacūrṇaṃ vā pūrvavat evaṃ kṣīreṇa
                        kāsaśvāsacchardikapharogeṣūpayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8"> dhāmārgavasyāpi madanaphalamajjavadupayogo
                        viśeṣatas tu garagulmodarakāsaśvāsaśleṣmāmayeṣu vāyau ca
                        kaphasthānagate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9"> kṛtavedhanaphalapippalīnāṃ
                        vamanadravyakaṣāyaparipītānāṃ bahuśaś cūrṇamutpalādiṣu dattam
                        āghrātaṃ vāmayati tattvanavabaddhadoṣeṣu yavāgūm ākaṇṭhāt
                        pītavatsu ca vidadhyāt | vamanavirecanaśirovirecanadravyāṇy evaṃ
                        vā pradhānatamāni bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.10"> bhavataś cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanadravyayogāṇāṃ dig iyaṃ saṃprakīrtitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāṃ vibhajya yathāvyādhi kālaśaktiviniścayāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.11"> kaṣāyaiḥ svarasaiḥ kalkaiś cūrṇair api ca
                        buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         peyalehyādyabhojyeṣu vamanāny upakalpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyo nāma tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||
                    </l>
                </div>



                <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.1"> athāto virecanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.3"> aruṇābhaṃ trivṛnmūlaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mūlavirecane |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradhānaṃ tilvakas tvakṣu phaleṣv api harītakī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.4"> taileṣv eraṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ svarase kāravellikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudhāpayaḥ payaḥsūktam iti prādhānyasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.5"> vairecanadravyarasānupītaṃ mūlaṃ
                        mahattraivṛtamastadoṣam |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇīkṛtam saindhavanāgarāḍhyamamlaiḥ pibenmārutarogajuṣṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.6"> ikṣorvikārair madhurai rasais tat paitte gade
                        kṣīrayutaṃ pibec ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         guḍūcyariṣṭatriphalārasena savyoṣamūtraṃ kaphaje pibet tat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.7"> trivarṇakatryūṣaṇayuktam etad guḍena lihyād
                        anavena cūrṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthe ca tanmūlarasasya dattvā tanmūlakalkaṃ kuḍavapramāṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.8"> karṣonmite saindhanāgare ca vipācya kalkīkṛtam
                        etad adyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatkalkabhāgaḥ samahauṣadhārdhaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayutaś ca peyaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.9"> samāstrivṛnnāgarakābhayāḥ syurbhāgārdhakaṃ
                        pūgaphalaṃ supakvam |
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgasāro maricaṃ sadāru yogaḥ sasindhūdbhavamūtrayuktaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.10"> virecanadravyabhavaṃ tu cūrṇaṃ rasena teṣāṃ
                        bhiṣajā vimṛdya |
                        <caesura/>
                         tanmūlasiddhena ca sarpiṣā+āktaṃ sevyaṃ tadājye guṭikīkṛtaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.11"> guḍe ca pākābhimukhe nidhāya cūrṇīkṛtaṃ
                        samyagidaṃ vipācya |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītaṃ trijātāktamatho vimṛdya yogānurūpā guṭikāḥ prayogyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.12"> vairekīyadravyacūrṇasya bhāgaṃ siddhaṃ sārdhaṃ
                        kvāthabhāgaiś caturbhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmṛdnīyāt sarpiṣā tacchṛtena tatkvāthoṣmasveditaṃ sāmitaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.13"> pākaprāpte phāṇite cūrṇitaṃ tat kṣiptaṃ pakvaṃ

                        <caesura/>
                         śītībhūtā modakā hṛdyagandhāḥ kāryāstvete bhakṣyakalpāḥ samāsāt
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.14"> rasena teṣāṃ paribhāvya mudgān yūṣaḥ
                        sasindhūdbhavasarpiriṣṭaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vairecane 'nyair api vaidalaiḥ syādevaṃ vidadhyādvamanauṣadhaiś
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.15"> bhittvā dvidhekṣuṃ parilipya kalkais
                        tribhaṇḍijātaiḥ pratibadhya rajjvā |

                        <caesura/>
