                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.44"> jñātvā jātarasaṃ cāpi tat tuṣodakam ādiśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tuṣāmbusauvīrakayor vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.45"> ṣaḍrātrāt saptarātrād vā te ca peye prakīrtite
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         vairecaneṣu sarveṣu trivṛnmūlavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.46"> dantīdravantyor mūlāni viśeṣān mṛtkuśāntare |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīkṣaudrayutkāni svinnāny uddhṛtya śoṣayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.47"> tatas trivṛdvidhānena yojayec chleṣmapittayoḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tayoḥ kalkakaṣāyābhyāṃ cakratailaṃ vipācayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.48"> sarpiś ca pakvaṃ vīsarpakakṣād āhāla jīrjayet
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         mehagulmānilaśleṣmavibandhāṃstailam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.49"> catuḥsnehaṃ śakṛcchukravātasaṃrodhajā rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dantīdravantīmaricakanakāhvayavāsakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.50"> viśvabheṣajamṛdvīkācitrakair mūtrabhāvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         saptāhaṃ sarpiṣā cūrṇaṃ yojyam etad virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.51"> jīrṇe santarpaṇaṃ kṣaudraṃ
                        pittaśleṣmarujāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajīrṇapārśvarukpāṇḍuplīhodaranibarhaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.52"> guḍasyāṣṭapale pathyā viṃśatiḥ syuḥ palaṃ
                        palam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dantīcitrakayoḥ karṣau pippalītrivṛtordaśa || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.53"> kṛtvaitān modakān ekaṃ daśame daśame 'hani |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ khāded uṣṇatoyasevī niryantraṇās tv ime || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.54ab"> doṣaghnā grahaṇīpāṇḍurogārśaḥkuṣṭhanāśanāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.54cd"> vyoṣaṃ trijātakaṃ mustā viḍaṅgāmalake tathā
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.55"> navaitāni samāṃśāni trivṛdaṣṭaguṇāni vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇacūrṇīkṛtānīha dantībhāgadvayaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.56ab"> sarvāṇi cūrṇitānīha gālitāni vimiśrayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.56cd"> ṣaḍbhiś ca śarkarābhāgair
                        īṣatsaindhavamākṣikaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.57ab"> piṇḍitam bhakṣayitvā tu tataḥ śītāmbu
                        pāyayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.57cd"> bastiruktṛḍjvaracchardiśoṣapāṇḍubhramāpaham
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.58ab"> niryantraṇam idaṃ sarvaṃ viṣaghnaṃ tu
                        virecanam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.58cd"> trivṛdaṣṭakasaṃjño 'yaṃ praśastaḥ
                        pittarogiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.59"> bhakṣyaḥ kṣīrānupāno vā pittaśleṣmāturair
                        naraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhakṣyarūpasadharmatvād āḍhyeṣv eva vidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.60"> tilvaksya tvacaṃ bāhyām antar valkavivarjitām
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇayitvā tu dvau bhāgau tat kaṣāyeṇa gālayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.61"> tṛtīyaṃ bhāvitaṃ tena bhāgaṃ śuṣkaṃ tu
                        bhāvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśamūlīkaṣāyeṇa trivṛdvatsaṃprayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.62"> vidhānaṃ tvakṣu nirdiṣṭaṃ phalānām atha
                        vakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         harītakyāḥ phalaṃ tv asthivimuktaṃ doṣavarjitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.63"> yojyaṃ trivṛdvidhānena sarvavyādhinibarhaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanaṃ paraṃ medhyaṃ duṣṭāntarvraṇaśodhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.64"> harītakī viḍaṅgāni saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ trivṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         maricāni ca tat sarvaṃ gomūtreṇa virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.65"> harītakī bhadradāru kuṣṭhaṃ pūgaphalaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ ca gomūtreṇa virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.66"> nīlinīphalacūrṇaṃ ca nāgarābhayayos tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyād guḍena salilaṃ paścāduṣṇaṃ piben naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.67"> pippalyādikaṣāyeṇa pibet piṣṭāṃ harītakīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavopahitāṃ sadya eṣa yogo virecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.68"> harītakī bhakṣyamāṇā nāgareṇa guḍena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saidhavopahitā vā 'pi sātatyenāgnidīpanī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.69"> vātānulomanī vṛṣyā cendriyāṇāṃ prasādanī |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarpaṇakṛtān rogān prāyo hanti harītakī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.70"> śītam āmalakaṃ rūkṣaṃ pittamedaḥkaphāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         bibhītakam anuṣṇaṃ tu kaphapittanibarhaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.71ab"> trīṇy apy amlakaṣāyāṇi satiktamadhurāṇi ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.71cd"> triphalā sarvarogaghnī
                        tribhāgaghṛtamūrcchitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.72ab"> vayasaḥ sthāpanaṃ cāpi kuryāt saṃtatasevitā
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.72cd"> harītakīvidhānena phalāny evaṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.73"> virecanāni sarvāṇi viśeṣāccaturaṅgulāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalaṃ kāle samuddhṛtya sikatāyāṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.74"> saptāham ātape śuṣkaṃ tato majjānam uddharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ grāhyaṃ jale paktvā tilavad vā prapīḍya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.75"> tasyopayogo bālānāṃ yāvad varṣāṇi dvādaśa |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyād eraṇḍatailena kuṣṭhatrikaṭukānvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.76"> sukhodakaṃ cānupibedeṣa yogo virecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         eraṇḍatailaṃ triphalākvāthena triguṇena tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.77"> yuktaṃ pītaṃ tathā kṣīrarasābhyāṃ tu virecayet
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇasukumāreṣu yojitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.78"> phalānāṃ vidhir uddiṣṭaḥ kṣīrāṇāṃ śṛṇu suśruta
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanānāṃ tīkṣṇānāṃ payaḥ saudhaṃ paraṃ matam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.79"> ajñaprayuktaṃ tad dhanti viṣavat
                        karmavibhramāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         vijānatā prayuktaṃ tu mahāntam api saṃcayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.80"> bhinatty āśveva doṣāṇāṃ rogān hanti ca
                        dustarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahatyāḥ pañcamūlyāstu bṛhatyoś caikaśaḥ pṛthak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.81"> kaṣāyaiḥ samabhāgaṃ tu tadaṅgārair viśoṣitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         amlādimiḥ pūrvavat tu prayojyaṃ kolasaṃmitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.82"> mahāvṛkṣapayaḥ pītair yavāgūstaṇḍulaiḥ kṛtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītā virecayatyāśu guḍenotkārikā kṛtā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.83"> leho vā sādhitaḥ samyak snuhīkṣīrapayoghṛtaiḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhāvitās tu snuhīkṣīre pippalyo lavaṇānvitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.84ab"> cūrṇaṃ kāmpillakaṃ vā'pi tatpītaṃ
                        guṭikīkṛtam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.84cd"> saptalā śaṅkhinī dantī trivṛdāragvadhaṃ
                        gavām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.85"> mūtreṇāplāvya saptāhaṃ snuhīkṣīre tataḥ param
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         kīrṇaṃ tenaiva cūrṇena mālyaṃ vasanam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86ab"> āghrāyāvṛtya vā samyaṅnṛdukoṣṭho viricyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86cd"> kṣīratvakadphalamūlānāṃ vidhānaiḥ
                        parikīrtitaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86ef"> avekṣya samyag rogādīn yathāvad upayojayet
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.87"> trivṛcchāṇamitāstisrastisraś ca triphalātvacaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgapippalīkṣaraśāṇāstisraś ca cūrṇitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.88"> lihyāt sarpirmadhubhyāṃ ca modakaṃ vā guḍena
                        vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhakṣayen niṣparīhārametacchreṣṭhaṃ virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.89"> gulmān plīhodaram kāsaṃ halīmakamarocakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphavātakṛtāṃś cānyān vyādhīn etad vyapohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.90"> ghṛteṣu taileṣu payaḥsu cāpi madyeṣu mūtreṣu
                        tathā raseṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhakṣyānnalehyeṣu ca teṣu teṣu virecanāny agramatir vidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.91"> kṣīraṃ rasaḥ kalkam atho kaṣāyaḥ śṛtaś ca
                        śītaś ca tathaiva phāṇṭam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalpāh ṣaḍete khalu bheṣajānāṃ yathottaraṃ te laghavaḥ pradiṣṭāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        virecanadravyaviklpavijñānīyo nāma catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||
                    </l>
                </div>



                <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.1"> athāto dravadravyavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3"> pānīyamāntarīkṣamanirdeśyarasamamṛtaṃ jīvaṇaṃ
                        tarpaṇaṃ dhāraṇamāśvāsajananaṃ
                        śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrānidrādāhapraśamanamekāntataḥ
                        pathyatamaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4"> tad evāvanipatitam anyatamaṃ rasam upalabhate
                        sthānaviśeṣān
                        nadīnadasarastaḍāgavāpīkūpacuṇṭīprasravaṇodbhidavikirakedārapalvalādiṣu
                        sthāneṣv avasthitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5"> tatra lohitakapilapāṇḍunīlapītaśukleṣv
                        avanipradeśeṣu madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyāṇi yathāsaṅkhyam
                        udakāni saṃbhavantīty eke bhāṣante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6"> tat tu na samyak | tatra pṛthivyādīnām
                        anyonyānupraveśakṛtaḥ salilaraso bhavaty uktarṣāpakarṣeṇa | tatra
                        svalakṣaṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmāvamlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        madhuraṃ tejoguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṭukaṃ tiktaṃ ca
                        vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṣāyaṃ ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāmavyaktarasaṃ
                        avyaktaṃ hy ākāśam ity ataḥ tat pradhānam avyaktarasatvāt tat
                        peyam āntarīkṣalābhe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7"> tatrāntarīkṣaṃ caturvidham | tadyāthā dhāraṃ
                        kāraṃ tauṣāraṃ haimam iti | teṣāṃ dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ laghutvāt tat
                        punar dvividhaṃ gāṅgaṃ sāmudraṃ ceti | tatra gāṅgam āśvayuje māsi
                        prāyaśo varṣati | tayor dvayor api parīkṣaṇaṃ kurvīta
                        śālyodanapiṇḍam akuthitam avidagdhaṃ rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati
                        deve bahiṣkurvīta sa yadi muhūrtam sthitastādṛśa eva bhavati tadā
                        gāṅgaṃ patatīty avagantavyaṃ varṇānyatve sikthapraklede ca
                        sāmudram iti vidyāt tan nopādeyam | sāmudram apy āśvayuje māsi
                        gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavad bhavati | gāṅgaṃ punaḥ pradhānaṃ tad
                        upādadītāśvayuje māsi | śuciśuklavitatapaṭaikadeśacyutam athavā
                        harmyatalaparibhraṣṭam anyair vā śucibhir bhājanair gṛhītaṃ
                        sauvarṇe rajate mṛnmaye vā pātre nidadhyāt | tat sarvakālam
                        upayuñjīta tasyālābhe bhaumam | tac cākāśaguṇabahulam | tat punaḥ
                        saptavidham | tadyathā kaupaṃ nādeyaṃ sārasaṃ tāḍāgaṃ prāsravaṇaṃ
                        audbhidaṃ cauṇṭyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8"> tatra varṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhidaṃ vā seveta
                        mahāguṇatvāt śaradi sarvaṃ prasannatvāt hemante sārasaṃ tāḍāgaṃ vā
                        vasante kaupaṃ prāsravaṇaṃ vā grīṣme 'py evaṃ prāvṛṣi cauṇṭyam
                        anabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9"> kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśavakothapradūṣitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṇaparṇotkarayutaṃ kaluṣaṃ viṣasaṃ yutam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10"> yo 'vagāheta varṣāsu pibed vāpi navaṃ jalam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bāhyābhyantarān rogān prāpnuyāt kṣipram eva tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11"> tatra yat
                        paṅkaśaivalahaṭatṛṇapadmapatraprabhṛtibhir avacchannaṃ
                        śaśisūryakiraṇānilair nābhijuṣṭaṃ gandhavarṇarasopasṛṣṭaṃ ca tad
                        vyāpannam iti vidyāt | tasya sparśarūparasagandhavīryavipākadoṣāḥ
                        ṣaṭ saṃbhavanti | tatra kharatā paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ dantagrāhitā
                        ca sparśadoṣaḥ paṅkasikatāśaivālabbahuvarṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ
                        vyaktarasatā rasadoṣaḥ aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ yad upayuktaṃ
                        tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekān āpādayati sa vīryadoṣaḥ yad
                        upayuktaṃ cirād vipacyate viṣṭambhayati vā sa vipākadoṣa iti | ta
                        ete āntarikṣe na santi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12"> vyāpannasya cāgnikvathanaṃ sūryātapapratāpanaṃ
                        taptāyaḥpiṇḍasikatāloṣṭrāṇāṃ vā nirvāpaṇaṃ prasādanaṃ ca kartavyaṃ
                        nāgacampakotpalapāṭalāpuṣpaprabhṛtibhiś cādhivāsanam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.13"> sauvarṇe rājate tāmre kāṃsye maṇimaye 'pi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         puṣpāvataṃsaṃ bhaume vā sugandhi salilaṃ pibet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.14"> vyāpannaṃ varjayennityaṃ toyaṃ
                        yaccāpyanārtavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣasaṃjananaṃ hyetannādadītāhitaṃ tu tat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.15"> vyāpannam salilaṃ yastu pibatīhāprasādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvayathuṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca tvagdoṣamavipākatām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.16"> śvāsakāsapratiśyāyaśūlagulmodarāṇi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyānvā viṣamānrogānprāpnuyādacireṇa saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.17"> tatra sapta kaluṣasya prasādanāni bhavanti |
                        tadyathā katakagomedakabisagranthiśaivālamūlavastrāṇi muktāmaṇiś
                        ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.18"> pañca nikṣepaṇāni bhavanti | tadyathā phalakaṃ
                        tryaṣṭakaṃ muñjavalaya udakamañcikā śikyaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.19"> sapta śītīkaraṇāni bhavanti pravātasthāpanaṃ
                        udakaprakṣepaṇaṃ yaṣṭikābhrāmaṇaṃ vyajanaṃ vastroddharaṇaṃ
                        vālukāprakṣepaṇaṃ śikyāvalambanaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.20"> nirgandhamavyaktarasaṃ tṛṣṇāghnaṃ śuci śītalam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         acchaṃ laghu ca hṛdyaṃ ca toyaṃ guṇavaducyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.21"> tatra nadyaḥ paścimābhimukhāḥ pathyāḥ
                        laghūdakatvāt pūrvābhimukhās tu na praśasyante gurūdakatvāt
                        dakṣiṇābhimukhā nā'tidoṣalāḥ sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra sahyaprabhavāḥ
                        kuṣṭhaṃ janayanti vindhyaprabhavāḥ kuṣṭhaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca
                        malayaprabhavāḥ kṛmīn mahendraprabhavāḥ ślīpadodarāṇi
                        himavatprabhavā hṛdrogaśvayathuśirorogaślīpadagalagaṇḍān
                        prācyāvantyā aparāvantyāś cārśāṃsyupajanayanti pāriyātraprabhavāḥ
                        pathyā balārogyakarya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.22"> nadyaḥ śīghravahā laghvyaḥ proktā yāś
                        cāmalodakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurvyaḥ śaivālasaṃcchannāḥ kaluṣā mandagāś ca yāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.23"> prāyeṇa nadyo maruṣu satiktā lavaṇānvitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghvyaḥ samadhurāś caiva pauruṣeyā bale hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.24"> tatra sarveṣāṃ bhaumānāṃ grahaṇaṃ pratyūṣasi
                        tatra hy amalatvaṃ śaityaṃ cādhikaṃ bhavati sa eva cāpāṃ paro guṇa
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.25"> divārkakiraṇair juṣṭaṃ niśāyām induraśmibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         arūkṣam anabhiṣyandi tat tulyaṃ gaganāmbunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.26"> gaganāmbu tridoṣaghnaṃ gṛhītaṃ yat subhājane |
                        <caesura/>
                         balyaṃ rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ pātrāpekṣi tataḥ param || </l>

                         hanti kāreṇavaṃ sarpiḥ kaphakuṣṭhaviṣakrimīn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.105"> kṣīraghṛtaṃ punaḥ saṃgrāhi
                        raktrapittabhramamūrcchāpraśamanaṃ netrarogahitaṃ ca || </l>

                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.112">atha tailāni | tailaṃ tvāgneyamuṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ

                        medhāmārdavamāṃsasthairyavarṇabalakaraṃ cakṣuṣyaṃ baddhamūtraṃ
                        lekhanaṃ tiktakaṣāyānurasaṃ pācanam anilabalāsakṣayakaraṃ
                        krimighnam aśitapittajananaṃ yoniśiraḥkarṇaśūlapraśamanaṃ

                        ca pariṣekābhyaṅgāvagāhādiṣu tilatailaṃ praśasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.113"> tad bastiṣu ca pāneṣu nasye karṇākṣipūraṇe |

                <div n="46" type="adhyāya">

                    <head> ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1"> athāto 'nnapānavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3"> dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca
                        prāgabhihitaḥ prāṇināṃ punar mūlam āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa
                        ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattaḥ rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayiṇaḥ
                        dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī doṣāṇāṃ sāmyaṃ ca
                        brahmāder api ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthityutpattivināśahetuḥ
                        āhārādevābhivṛddhir balam ārogyaṃ varṇendriyaprasādaś ca tathā hy
                        āhāravaiṣamyād asvāsthyaṃ tasyāśitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpasyānekavidhaprabhāvasya pṛthak
                        pṛthag dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākaprabhāvakarmāṇīcchāmi jñātuṃ na hy
                        anavabuddhasvabhāvā bhiṣajaḥ svasthānuvṛttiṃ roganigrahaṇaṃ ca
                        kartuṃ samarthāḥ āhārāyattāś ca sarvaprāṇino yasmāt tasmād
                        annapānavidhim upadiśatu me bhagavān ity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ atha khalu vatsa suśruta yathāpraśnam ucyamānam
                        upadhārayasva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4"> tatra
                        lohitaśālikalamakardamakapāṇḍukasugandhakaśakunāhṛtapuṣpāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukarodhrapuṣpakadīrghaśūkakāñcanakamahiṣamahāśūkahāyanakadūṣakamahādūṣakaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        śālayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5"> madhurā vīryataḥ śītā laghupākā balāvahāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaghnālpānilakaphāḥ snigdhā baddhālpavarcasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6"> teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuṣyo varṇabalakṛt svaryo hṛdyastṛṣāpahaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7"> vraṇyo jvaraharaś caiva sarvadoṣaviṣāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo 'varāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8">
                        ṣaṣṭikakāṅgukamukundakapītakapramodakakākalakāsanapuṣpakamahāṣaṣṭikacūrṇakakuravakakedāraprabhṛtayaḥ
                        ṣaṣṭikāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9"> rase pāke ca madhurāḥ śamanā vātapittayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śālīnāṃ ca guṇais tulyā bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphaśukralāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10"> ṣadṣtikaḥ pravarsteṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛduḥ snigdhastridoṣaghnaḥ sthairyakṛdvalavardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11"> vipāke madhuro grāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣāstvalpāntaraguṇāḥ ṣaṣṭikāḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12">
                        kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhajatumukhanandīmukhalāvākṣakatvaritakakukkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭakaprabhṛtayo
                        vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke 'madhurā vīryato 'himāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpābhiṣyandinas tulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikaribaddhavarcasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14"> kṛṣṇavrīhir varas teṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśo vrīhayo 'pare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15"> dagdhāyāmavanau jātāḥ śālayo laghupākinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyā baddhaviṇmūtrā rūkṣāḥ śleṣmāpakarṣaṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.16"> sthalajāḥ kaphapittaghnāḥ kaṣāyāḥ kaṭukānvayāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiṃcitsatiktamadhurāḥ pavanānalavardhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.17"> kaidārā madhurā vṛṣyā balyāḥ pittanibarhaṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         īṣatkaṣāyālpamalā guravaḥ kaphaśukralāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.18"> ropyātiropyā laghavaḥ śīghrapākā guṇottarāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         adāhino doṣaharā balyā mūtravivardhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.19"> śālayaś chinnarūḍhā ye rūkṣāste baddhavarcasaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiktāḥ kaṣāyāḥ pittaghnā laghupākāḥ kaphāpahāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.20"> vistareṇāyam uddiṣṭaḥ śālivargo hitāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadvat kudhānyamudgādimāṣādīnāṃ ca vakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.21"> atha kudhānyavargaḥ |
                        koradūṣakaśyāmākanīvāraśāntanuvarakoddālakapriyaṅgumadhūlikānāndīmukhīkuruvindagavedhukasarabarukatoda(?ya)parṇīmukundakaveṇuyavaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        kudhānyaviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.22"> uṣṇāḥ kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmaghnā baddhanisyandā vātapittaprakopaṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.23"> kāṣayamadhuras teṣāṃ śītaḥ pittāpahaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kodravaś ca sanīvāraḥ śyāmākaś ca saśāntanuḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.24"> kṛṣṇā raktāś ca pītāś ca śvetāś caiva
                        priyaṅgavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathottaram pradhānāḥ syū rūkṣāḥ kaphaharāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.25"> madhūlī madhurā śītā snigdhā nandīmukhī tathā
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśoṣī tatra bhūyiṣṭhaṃ varukaḥ samukundakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.26"> rūkṣā veṇuyavā jñeyā vīryoṣṇāḥ kaṭupākinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         baddhamūtrāḥ kaphaharāḥ kaṣāyā vātakopanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.27">
                        mudgavanamudgakalāyamakuṣṭhamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakasatīnatripuṭakahareṇvāḍhakīprabhṛtayo
                        vaidalāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.28"> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītāḥ kaṭupākā marutkarāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         baddhamūtrapurīṣāś ca pittaśleṣmaharās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.29"> nātyarthaṃ vātalās teṣu mudgā dṛṣṭiprasādanaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradhānā haritās tatra vanyā mudgasamāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.30"> vipāke madhurāḥ proktā masūrā baddhavarcasaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         makuṣṭhakāḥ kṛmikarāḥ kalāyāḥ pracurānilāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.31"> āḍhakī kaphapittaghnī nātivātaprakopaṇī |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātalāḥ śītamadhurāḥ sakaṣāyā virūkṣaṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.32"> kaphaśoṇitapittaghnāś caṇakāḥ puṃstvanāśanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ta eva ghṛtasaṃyuktāstridoṣaśamanāḥ param || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.33"> hareṇavaḥ satīnāś ca vijñeyā baddhavarcasaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛte mudgamasūrābhyām anye tvādhmānakārakāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34"> māṣo gururbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdhoṣṇavṛṣyo
                        madhuro 'nilaghnaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarpaṇaḥ stnayakaro viśeṣādbalapradaḥ śukrakaphāvahaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35"> kaṣāyabhāvānna purīṣabhedī na mūtralo naiva
                        kaphasya kartā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svādurvipāke madhuro 'lasāndraḥ santarpaṇaḥ stanyarucipradaś ca
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36"> māṣaiḥ samānaṃ phalamātmaguptamuktaṃ ca
                        kākāṇḍaphalaṃ tathaiva |
                        <caesura/>
                         āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37"> uṣṇaḥ kulattho rasataḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭurvipāke
                        kaphamārutaghnaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śukrāśmarīgulmaniṣūdanaś ca sāṃgrāhikaḥ pīnasakāsahārī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38"> ānāhamedogudakīlahikkāśvāsāpahaḥ
                        śoṇitapittakṛc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphasya hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39"> īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ satiktaḥ sāṃgrāhikaḥ
                        pittarakarastathoṣṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilo vipāke madhuro baliṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇālepana eva pathyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40"> dantyo 'gnimedhājanano 'lpamūtrastvacyo 'tha
                        keśyo 'nilahā guruś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tileṣu sarveṣv asitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarās tathā'nye
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41"> yavaḥ kaṣāyo madhuro himaś ca kaṭurvipāke
                        kaphapittahārī |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣu pathyastilavacca nityaṃ prabaddhamūtro bahuvātavarcāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42"> sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇakṛc ca sapicchilaḥ
                        sthūlavilekhanaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         medomaruttṛḍ{ṃ.-}haraṇo 'tirūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ śoṇitapittayoś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43"> ebhir guṇair hīnatarais tu
                        kiṃcidvidyādyavebhyo 'tiyavānaśeṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         godhūma ukto madhuro guruś ca balyaḥ sthiraḥ śukrarucipradaś ca
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44"> snigdho 'tiśīto 'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛt
                        śleṣmakaraḥ saraś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśoṣaśukrabalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45"> kaṭurvipāke madhuras tu śimbaḥ
                        prabandhaviṇmārutapittalaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sitāsitāḥ pītakaraktavarṇā bhavanti ye 'nekavidhās tu śimbāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46"> yathoditāste guṇataḥ pradhānā jñeyāḥ kaṭūṣṇā
                        rasapākayoś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahādvayaṃ mūlakajāś ca śimbāḥ kuśimbivallīprabhavās tu śimbāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47"> jñeyā vipāke madhurā rase ca balapradāḥ
                        pittanibarhaṇāś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidāhavantaś ca bhṛśaṃ virūkṣā viṣṭabhya jīryantyanilapradāś ca
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48"> rucipradāś caiva sudurjarāś ca sarve smṛtā
                        vaidalikās tu śimbāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭurvipāke kaṭukaḥ kaphaghno vidāhibhāvādahitaḥ kusumbaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49"> uṣṇā'tasī svādurasā'nilaghnī pittolbaṇā syāt
                        kaṭukā vipāke |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāke rase cāpi kaṭuḥ pradiṣṭaḥ siddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49ef"> tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣaḥ kaphamārutaghnas tathāguṇaś
                        cāsitasarṣapo 'pi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.50"> anārtavaṃ vyādhihatamaparyāgatam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhūmijaṃ navaṃ cāpi na dhānyaṃ guṇavat smṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.51"> navaṃ dhānyam abhiṣyandi laghu saṃvatsaroṣitam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidāhi guru viṣṭambhi virūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭidūṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52"> śālyādeḥ sarṣapāntasya vividhasyāsya bhāgaśaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         kālapramāṇasaṃskāramātrāḥ saṃparikīrtitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53"> athordhvaṃ māṃsavargān upadekṣyāmaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā jaleśayā ānūpā grāmyāḥ kravyabhuja ekaśaphā jāṅgalāś
                        ceti ṣaṇmāṃsavargāḥ | eteṣāṃ vargāṇāmuttarottaraṃ pradhānatamāḥ |
                        te punardvividhājāṅgalā ānūpāś ceti | tatra jāṅgalavargo
                        'ṣṭavidhaḥ | tad yathā jaṅghālā viṣkirāḥ pratudā guhāśayāḥ
                        prasahāḥ parṇamṛgā bileśayā grāmyāś ceti | teṣaṃ jaṅghālaviṣkirau
                        pradhānatamau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54"> tāv
                        eṇahariṇarkṣakuraṅgakarālakṛtamālaśarabhaśvadaṃṣṭrāpṛṣatacāruṣkaramṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayo
                        jaṅghālā mṛgāḥ kaṣāyā madhurā laghavo vātapittaharās tīkṣṇā hṛdyā
                        bastiśodhanāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55"> kaṣāyo madhuro hṛdyaḥ pittāsṛkkapharogahā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃgrāhī rocano balyas teṣām eṇo jvarāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56"> madhuro madhuraḥ pāke doṣaghno 'naladīpanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalo baddhaviṇmūtraḥ sugandhirhariṇo laghuḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.57ab"> eṇaḥ kṛṣṇas tayor jñeyo hariṇas tāmra ucyate
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.57cd"> yo na kṛṣṇo na tāmraś ca kuraṅgaḥ so
                        'bhidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.58"> śītā'sṛkpittaśamanī vijñeyā mṛgamātṛkā |
                        <caesura/>

                        viṣkirāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60"> laghavaḥ śītamadhurāḥ kaṣāyā doṣanāśanāḥ |

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.61"> īṣadgurūṣṇamadhuro vṛṣyo medhāgnivardhanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.64"> laghavaḥ krakarā hṛdyās tathā caivopacakrakāḥ

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        tu saḥ | </l>

                        kapotapārāvatabhṛṅgarājaparabhṛtakoyaṣṭikakuliṅgagṛhakuliṅgagokṣveḍakaḍiṇḍimāṇavakaśatapatrakamātṛnindakabhedāśiśukasārikāvalgulīgiriśālaṭvālaṭṭūṣakasugṛhākhañjarīṭahārītadātyūhaprabhṛtayaḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.116"> pāṭhīnaḥ śleṣmalo vṛṣyo nidrāluḥ piśitāśanaḥ

                        <caesura/>
                         dūṣayed raktapittaṃ tu kuṣṭharogaṃ karotyasau |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432"> tatra pūrvaśasyajātīnāṃ badarāmlaṃ vaidalānāṃ
                        dhānyāmlaṃ jaṅghālānāṃ dhanvajānāṃ ca pippalyāsavaḥ viṣkirāṇāṃ
                        kolabadarāsavaḥ pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛkṣāsavaḥ guhāśayānāṃ
                        kharjūranālikerāsavaḥ prasahānāmaśvagandhāsavaḥ parṇamṛgāṇāṃ
                        kṛṣṇagandhāsavaḥ bileśayānāṃ phalasārāsavaḥ ekaśaphānāṃ
                        triphalāsavaḥ anekaśaphānāṃ khadirāsavaḥ kūlacarāṇāṃ
                        śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukāsavaḥ kośavāsināṃ pādināṃ ca sa eva plavānām
                        ikṣurasāsavaḥ nādeyānāṃ matsyānāṃ mṛṇālāsavaḥ sāmudrāṇāṃ tu
                        mātuluṅgāsavaḥ amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ kaṣāyāṇāṃ
                        dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khaṇḍāsavaḥ
                        tālaphalādīnāṃ dhanyāmlaṃ kaṭukānāṃ dūrvānalavetrāsavaḥ
                        pippalyādīnāṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ kūṣmāṇḍādīnāṃ dārvīkarīrāsavaḥ
                        cuccuprabhṛtīnāṃ lodhrāsavaḥ jīvantyādīnāṃ triphalāsavaḥ
                        kusumbhaśākasya sa eva maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnāṃ mahāpañcamūlāsavaḥ
                        tālamastakādīnām amlaphalāsavaḥ saindhavādīnāṃ surāsava āranālaṃ
                        ca toyaṃ vā sarvatreti || </l>

                         klinnavisrastadhātutvād ajīrṇe na hitaṃ divā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530"> imaṃ vidhiṃ yo 'numataṃ mahāmuner
                        nṛparṣimukhyasya paṭhed dhi yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bhūmipālāya vidhātum auṣadhaṃ mahātmanāṃ cārhati sūrisattamaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ
                        tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā suśrutena viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ
                        sūtrasthāne ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</p>

                    <l ana="SS.1.46.trailer">samāptaṃ cedaṃ sūtrasthānam |</l>
                </div>

            </div>
        </body>
    </text>
</TEI>
